 jabaki aisa katai nahin he
 According to experts, good sleep can be made your partner even in the midst of a life of upheaval and all the turmoil
 jaankaar bataate hai ki sabase pehali jarurat yah he ki ham apane sone kii jagah ko comfortable banaaen
 Dark or light dim light can work
 1) lambii neend ko by-bijab kabhi sone kaa mauka mili to iskaa arth yah nahin he ki aap jarurat se zyada lambii neend len
 This interrupts you to sleep the next time
 saath hi kai sari bimariyon ko bhi aamantran detaa he
 2) Tea, coffee or energy drink Many people consume tea or coffee before bedtime
 garm doodh bhi acchhee neend laane main sahaayak hota he, lekin iske saath hi jaruri he ki aap dopaher main kya khate or pite hai iskaa dhyaan rakhaa jaae
 That is, it is better not to consume any energy drink after noon
 shaam chaar baje ek cap chaay aapke liye laabhakaari ho saktaa he
 3) Do not go to bed immediately after eating food before going to bed
 iske saath hi acchhee neend ke liye raat main halkaa bhojan len
 Overeating also creates problems for good sleep
 raat ke khaane main pasta, hari sabji, tamaato kaa soup, chikan aadi khaanaa acchhee neend ke liye laabhakaari he
 4) 'little' day-long fatigue before bedtime and after a light meal at night, wine or alcohol reduces your stress level
 gahari neend ke liye yah kaaphi madad karata he
 5) Bathing at night many people take bath just before bedtime
 kai iske liye garm pani kaa istemaal karte hai
 While bathing just before bedtime is an invitation to Anindra
 sone se pehle hamaara sharir ek nishchit taapmaana tak pahunchataa he, jabaki thik pehle snaan karne se isamen rukaawat paidaa hoti he
 6) Doing yoga just before bedtime or exercising right before sleeping, or less exhausting exercise or stretching can be beneficial for you
 aap is dauraan dimag ko shant karne ke liye meditation bhi kar sakate hai
 7) Everyone can have their own facility regarding the light and illumination of the room
 lekin sabase behatar hoga he ki aap kamare main maddham pili roshni rakhen
 If you like sleeping while reading a book, do not put a bulb with a light in the table light
 8) phone or tivijahan tak sambhav ho sone se pehle tivi or phone ko by-by kar den
 Many times people spend time on the phone, after which their sleep is blown away
 9) bedroom ko thik se lock kar lensone se pehle bedroom ko thik se lock kar len
 Not because someone will come into your room, but because doing so calms the mind and brings comfort
 10) din biit gaya, zyada na sochenkai log bistar par jane ke baad dinabhar kii ghatnaon or baton par soch-vichaar karne lagate hai
 this is wrong
